<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><b><span style="font-size:36.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;mso-ascii-color:#FF6600">唯识三十颂讲记</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:36.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-color:#FF6600"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span style="color:#003300">于凌波居士 讲述<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#003300">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a01">第一讲 唯识宗学统概述</a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#003300"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a02">第二讲 三十颂科判大纲</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a03">第三讲 唯识学上的几个基本概念</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a04">第四讲 识变——八识三能变</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:navy"><a href="#a05"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第五讲</span> <span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">异熟能变</span>——<span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第八识</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体;color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:navy"><a href="#a06"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第六讲</span> <span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">思量能变</span>——<span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">第七识</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体;color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a07">第七讲 了境能变——第六识</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a08">第八讲 前六识的王所相应至起灭分位</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a09">第九讲 正辨唯识与释违理难</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a10">第十讲 释违教难——三自性与三无性</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a11">第十一讲 明唯识性——真如</a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="center" style="text-align:center"><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"><a href="#a12">第十二讲 明唯识位——唯识五位修行</a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#003300"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a01"></a><span style="color:#333399">第一讲<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>唯识宗学统概述</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&lt;唯识三十颂&gt; ，是唯识宗的基本论典，唯识宗即依此论典而建立。所以要讲三十颂，必须要由唯识宗的建立与传承说起。中国的唯识宗，源自印度大乘佛教的瑜伽行学派。而说到瑜伽行学派，又不能不追溯到中观学派，兹依次介绍如下。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">一、 印度大乘佛教的中观与瑜伽二派</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">印度的大乘佛教，兴起于西元世纪开始之后。一代大哲龙树，住世年代约在西元一五零至二五零年之间，他出身于南印度的婆罗门种姓，自幼受婆罗门传统教育，后来皈依佛教。当时南印度已有大乘经典流行，他读之不以为走足，传说他游行北印度时，自雪山地区一个老比丘处得到一部分大乘经典，又在大龙族聚居之地得到许多大乘经典，这样就更充实了他的大乘理论。他回到南印度，把当时流行的般若思想组织起来，完成了<span lang="EN-US">‘缘起性空’的空宗哲学体系。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">原来龙树住世时代，印度思想界的潮流，一方面是外道的诸法实有、或常或断的思想，一方面是小乘有部的<span lang="EN-US">‘我空法有’，及‘法体恒有、三世实有’思想。龙树为破邪显正，他依据佛陀的根本思想缘起理论、及当时的般若思想，广造论典， 破斥邪说。 这种思想，表现在 &lt;中观论&gt; 一书中。如‘八不偈’所称：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">不生亦不灭，不常亦不断，不一亦不异，不来亦不出，</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">能说是因缘，善灭诸戏论，我稽首礼佛，诸说中第一。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">八不，其实就是全盘否定<span lang="EN-US">——自诸法空性上，否定小乘、外道的生灭、常断、一异、来出诸戏论。诸法以因缘和合而生，非独立存在，故无自性。无自性即‘性空’，亦曰 ‘空性’性，这一点则表现在‘三是偈’上。即所谓：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">诸因缘生法，我说即是空，亦为是假名，亦是中道义。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">龙树菩萨的著作很多，古有千部论主之称，除<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;中观论&gt; 外，主要的尚有 &lt;十二门论&gt; ， &lt;大智度论&gt; 等。继承龙树学说的，是他的弟子提婆。提婆所著的 &lt;百论&gt; ，与龙树的 &lt;中论&gt; 及 &lt;十二门论&gt; ，合称三论。是后来我国三论宗所依的论典。而龙树、提婆这一系的理论，在印度被称为 ‘中观学派’，亦称‘空宗]。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">龙树、提婆的空观，是以诸法无自性立论，并非徒持空见，妄计一切皆空。惟传至后世，则流为<span lang="EN-US">‘顽空’——学者不解空义，妄执一切皆空，于世俗谛，不施设有； 于胜义谛，真理亦无。此谓之‘恶取空’，亦称为‘沈空’。佛灭后九百年倾，无著、世亲两大论师出世，为矫治当时沈空之弊，而标示 ‘有’义。此有，非是小乘外道之诸法实有，而是破我法二执后所显示的‘真空妙有’。这在印度称为‘有宗’，亦称‘瑜伽行学派’。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">无著菩萨住世的年代，约为西元三六零至四六零年之间。据说天宫兜率内院的弥勒菩萨，应无著之请，在中印度阿瑜遮那国，为无著说<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 、 &lt;分别瑜伽论&gt; 、 &lt;大乘庄严论&gt; 、 &lt;辩中边论&gt; 、 &lt;金刚般若论&gt; 五部大论，无著承弥勒之说，与其弟世亲把五部大论做了一番综合整理工做，依此建立有宗，即印度的‘瑜伽行学派’。但弥勒不是历史上实有的人物，也许世间另有一个名叫弥勒的人。或者，五部大论根本是无著的著作，假托弥勒之名行世的。更可能的是，早在无著之前，就有许多无名的饱学的瑜伽师，而无著是继承他们学说而加以发扬的。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">无著梵名阿僧伽<span lang="EN-US"> Asaga、 是印度笈多王朝 (320—500) 中期的人，他是北印度健陀罗国富娄沙富城人，出身于婆罗门家庭，父名乔尸迦 Kausika、 居国师之位，有子三人，长即无著，次名世亲，幼名狮子觉。无著先在小乘佛教化地部出家，相传他因思惟空义不能得入，曾欲自杀，后得遇宾头罗罗汉为讲小乘空观，他初闻悟入，然犹不能满意，后来得到弥勒的五部大论，继承此说，集众宣之，由是大乘瑜伽法门传至四方。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">无著晚年游化于中天竺的乔赏弥国，百岁左右始入圆寂。他的著作很多，亦有千部论主之称。他所著的<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;显扬圣教论&gt; ，相当于 &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 的节略本； 而 在&lt;摄大乘论&gt;中已建立了唯识学的核心， &lt;大乘阿毗达摩集论&gt; 则是建立法相学的中心。无著的主要著作，有 &lt;显扬圣教论&gt; 、 &lt;摄大乘论&gt; 、 &lt;大乘阿毗达摩集论&gt; 、 &lt;大乘庄严经论&gt; 、 &lt;金刚般若论&gt; 、 &lt;能断金刚般若论颂&gt; 、 &lt;六门教授习定论颂&gt; 、<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;顺中论&gt; 等多种。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">世亲梵名<span lang="EN-US"> Vasabandhu、音译婆薮槃豆，是无著的异母弟，生卒年代约在西元三八零至四八零年间。陈代真谛译 &lt;婆薮槃豆法师传&gt; ，称他：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[于萨婆多部 (即说一切有部) 出家，博学多闻，遍通坟典，师才俊朗无可为俦，戒行清高，难以相匹。’ 据说世亲为了取舍阿毗达摩一系理论，他曾匿名化装，到有部的学术中心迦湿弥罗城，学习有部教理四年，后来回到富娄沙富城，用经量部教义，批判有部，集众宣说。且随讲随写，著为 &lt;阿毗达磨俱舍论 &gt; 。此论一出，颇有争论，而无能破之者，时人称此论为聪明论。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">世亲在北印度宣扬小乘，隐蔽大乘，其兄无著悯之，托以疾病，诱其来见，命弟子于邻室宣读<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;华严经、 十地品&gt; ，世亲闻之，方知其兄苦心。他深悔以往弘扬小乘诽谤大乘的错误，要割舌以谢过。无著对他说：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[你先前既用舌头诽谤大乘，现在何不用舌头来赞扬大乘呢？ ’这样世亲乃舍小入大，广造论释，宣扬大乘，而大成了唯识宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">世亲约于八十岁的时候，在阿瑜遮那国逝世，时其兄无著逝世已二十余年。他遗留的著作很多，与唯识学有关的，如下列所举<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;摄大乘论释&gt; 十卷，有三种译本，陈真谛译本名 &lt;摄大乘释论&gt; ，隋达摩笈多译本名 &lt;摄大乘论释论&gt; ，唐玄奘译本名 &lt;摄大乘论释&gt; 。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;辨中边论释&gt; 一卷，唐玄奘译。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;唯识二十颂&gt; 一卷，唐玄奘译。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;唯识三十颂&gt; 一卷，唐玄奘译。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;大乘五蕴论&gt; 一卷，唐玄奘译。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">六、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;百法明门论&gt; 一卷，唐玄奘译。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">印度古人造论，是先作本颂，总括全书要义，然后依颂作释，名曰长行，长行是论著的正文。而<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;唯识三十颂&gt; 一书，是世亲晚年之作，长行未作而已示寂。此际瑜伽行学派的理论已成为大乘佛教的主流，研究者极多，世亲寂后的百年之间，许多学者竞为三十多作释论，其中最著名者有十位，后世称为十大论师。十大论师的名字是：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 亲胜<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名畔徒室利，Bahbhu'sri， 与世亲同时。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 火辨<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名质旦罗婆拿 Citrabhana ，与世亲同时。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 德慧<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名娄拿末底 Gunamati ，他是安慧的老师。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 安慧<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名悉耻罗末底 Stharamati ，是大乘唯识宗有名的大学者。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、 难陀<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名 Nanda，意译欢喜。在唯识学心识上主张立相、见二分。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">六、 净月<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名质咀罗婆拿 Citrabhana ，与安慧同时。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">七、 护法<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名达磨波罗 Dharmapala ，六世纪中叶人。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">八、 胜友<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名毗世沙密多罗 Visesamitra， 曾在那烂陀寺从护法学唯识教义。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">九、 胜子<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名若那弗多罗 Jinaptra，著有 &lt;瑜伽师地论释&gt; 一卷，唐玄奘译。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">十、 智月<span lang="EN-US">： 梵名若那战多罗 Jnanacandra， 他也是护法的弟子。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">此处特别要介绍的是戒贤，他是西元六至七世间人。生于东印度三摩坦国，婆罗门种姓，少年好学，游历四方，访求名师，至中印度那烂陀寺，从护法受学出家，三十岁时，与南印度一大外道辩论获胜，受到国王的嘉赏，为他起造伽蓝。后来长期主持那烂陀寺，弘传唯识宗义，他依据<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;解深密经&gt; 、 &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 等经论，将佛教判为三时：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 第一时教：谓释尊初说阿含，说<span lang="EN-US">‘我空法有’之旨，称为有教。指小乘教。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 第二时教：谓释尊为大乘者说般若<span lang="EN-US">‘诸法皆空’之理，心境俱空，指大乘空宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 第三时教：谓释尊以三自性三无性之说，肯定非空非有之中道教，指大乘有宗。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">我国唐代玄奘三藏游学印度时，曾在那烂陀寺师事戒贤，依之学习<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 及十支论等唯识学说。时戒贤已一百零六岁为寺中大长老，众共尊称为正法藏。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">二、 中国唯识宗的建立</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">玄奘大师，是我国的四大译经家之一，也是唯识宗的开创人。他俗家姓陈、名褛，河南偃师人，隋文帝开皇二十年生。他有兄长捷<span lang="EN-US">， 早年在洛阳净土寺出家，玄奘亦于十三岁时随兄出家。唐高宗武德元年，与兄同入长安，寻赴成都参访。武德五年受具戒重回长安，从法常、僧辩二大德听 &lt;摄大乘论&gt; ，以诸师所说，各异宗途，圣典亦有隐晦，不知所从，乃欲西行天竺以明之。表请不许，奘师不为屈，乃就番人学书语，唐太宗贞观三年，私发长安，途中历经险阻，历时五年，始抵中天竺，于那烂陀寺，依戒贤论师学 &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 及十支论奥义五年。复从胜军居士学 &lt;唯识抉择论&gt; 及 &lt;庄严经论&gt; 等论典二年。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">奘师于贞观十九年回国，由天竺携回梵典六百五十余部，归国后广译经论，先后译出七十五部，一千三百余卷，其中关于法相唯识一系的，有下列各种<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;解深密经&gt; ： 五卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; ： 弥勒菩萨造，一百卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;辩中边论&gt; ： 弥勒菩萨造，三卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;摄大乘论&gt; ： 无著菩萨造，三卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;显扬圣教论&gt; ： 无著菩萨造，二十卷。 </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">六、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;大乘五蕴论&gt; ： 世亲菩萨造，一卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">七、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;大乘百法明门论&gt; ： 世亲菩萨造，一卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">八、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;瑜伽师地论释&gt; ： 世亲菩萨造，一卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">九、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;观所缘缘论&gt; ： 陈那论师造，一卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">十、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;唯识二十论&gt; ： 世亲菩萨造，一卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">十一、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;唯识三十论&gt; ： 世亲菩萨造，一卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">十二、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;成唯识论&gt; ： 以十大论师之释论百卷，揉集为识论十卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">由于玄奘广译法相唯识一系经论，窥基复弘扬之，开创了我国的唯识宗。除上述经论外，他也译出了小乘说一切有部的论典，如<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;阿毗达磨发智论&gt; 及六足论， &lt;大毗婆娑论&gt; 、 &lt;俱舍论&gt; 等。玄奘于唐高宗麟德元年示寂，享年六十五岁。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">玄奘大师的入室弟子窥基，俗姓尉迟，字洪道，是元魏尉迟部后裔，为唐初勋臣尉迟恭犹子，唐代京兆长安人。出生于唐太宗贞观六年，禀性聪慧，体貌魁伟，年十七岁奉敕出家，为玄奘弟子，依玄奘学佛教经论及天竺语文。二十五岁参与译经，唐高宗显庆四年，玄奘译<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;成唯识论&gt; ，原拟将十家释论各别全译，并命窥基与神[日＋方]、嘉尚、普光四人，分别担任检文、笔受、纂义工作，数日之后，窥基请求退出，奘师固问其故，基言：[群圣制作，各驰誉于五天，虽文具传于贝叶，而义不备于一本，情见各异，禀者无依，请错综群言，以为一本</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="mso-ascii-font-family:细明体">…</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">’。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">奘师乃礼遣三贤，窥基独任笔受，译出<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;成唯识论&gt; 十卷。其后奘师又为窥基阐说陈那之 &lt;因明正理门论&gt; ，及 &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 等，故窥基通达因明之学。窥基著述丰富，有[百部疏主’ 之称，其主要且与唯识有关者如有 &lt;瑜伽师地论略纂&gt; 十六卷， &lt;瑜伽论劫章颂&gt; ， &lt;成唯识论述记&gt; 二十卷， &lt;成唯识论掌中枢要&gt; 四卷， &lt;唯识二十论述记&gt; 三卷， &lt;大乘百法明门论解&gt; 一卷， &lt;成唯识论别钞&gt; 四卷， &lt;辩中边论述记&gt; 三卷， &lt;杂集论述记&gt; 十卷， &lt;因明入正理论疏&gt; 六卷， &lt;大乘法苑义林章&gt; 十四卷。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">由玄奘、窥基两代的弘扬，建立了我国大乘八宗之一的<span lang="EN-US">‘唯识宗’。唯识宗亦名法相宗、普为乘教宗、应理圆实宗、慈恩宗。由决判诸法体性相状故，名法相宗。由明万法唯识的妙理故，名唯识宗。由普为发趣一切乘者故，名普为乘教宗。由所谈的义理，均为圆满真实故，名应理圆实宗。由大唐慈恩寺玄奘、窥基二师所弘传故，名慈恩宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">窥基的弟子慧沼，淄州淄川<span lang="EN-US"> (今山东淄川) 人，生于唐高宗永徽二年，十五岁出家，曾亲炙玄奘法席，后转依窥基学唯识，深入堂奥。因为他住在淄川大云寺，故人称淄川大师。窥基示寂后，圆测著 &lt;成唯识识疏&gt; ，与窥基见解不同，慧沼撰 &lt;成唯识论了义灯&gt;破斥圆测之说，以显法相正义。他曾先后参加过义净、菩提流志的译场，担任正义，多所刊正。他的著作除 &lt;成唯识论了义灯&gt; 外，尚著有 &lt;能显中边慧日论&gt; 四卷、 &lt;因明入正理论义纂要&gt; 、 &lt;金刚般若经疏&gt; 、 &lt;金光明最胜王经疏&gt; 、 &lt;劝发菩提心集&gt; 等。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">智周是慧沼的弟子，濮阳人，唐高宗总章元年生。出家后初学天台，后师慧沼，著有<span lang="EN-US">&lt;成唯识论演秘&gt; 、 &lt;因明入正理论疏前记&gt; 三卷、 &lt;因明入正理论后记&gt; 三卷，及 &lt;大乘入道次第章&gt; 等十种。他的 &lt;成唯识论演秘&gt; ，与窥基的 &lt;枢要&gt; 及慧沼的 &lt;了义灯&gt;，合称为 &lt;唯识三疏&gt; 。智周的弟子如理，著有 &lt;成唯识论义演&gt; 及 &lt;成唯识论演秘释&gt;二书，唯内容则流于琐细。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">唯识宗建立后，宗风颇盛，百余年后，唐武宗<span lang="EN-US">‘会昌法难’兴起，此宗经疏大部焚毁，以后就日益式微了。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">三、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>唯识宗所依经论</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">唯识宗所依的经论，有所谓<span lang="EN-US">‘六经十一论’，及‘一本十支’之说。六经是： &lt;大方广佛华严经&gt; 、 &lt;解深密经&gt; 、 &lt;如来出现功德庄严经&gt; ：此经 中土未译。 &lt;阿毗达磨经&gt; ： 此经中土未译。 &lt;楞伽经&gt; 、 &lt;厚严经&gt; ： 此经中土未译。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">十一论是<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 、 &lt;显扬圣教论&gt; 、 &lt;大乘庄严经论&gt; 、 &lt;集量论&gt; 、 &lt;摄大乘论&gt; 、 &lt;十地经论&gt; 、 &lt;分别瑜伽论&gt; 、 &lt;辨中边论&gt; 、 &lt;二十唯识论&gt; 、 &lt;观所缘缘论&gt; 、 &lt;阿毗达磨杂集论&gt; 。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">以上六经十一论，在六经中，以<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;解深密经&gt; 为本经； 在十一论中，以 &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 为本论。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一本十支，又称<span lang="EN-US">‘十支论’，是以 &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 为本论，以百法、五蕴等十种论典为支论的名称，这是研究唯识学必读的论典，十支论的名称如下：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 略陈名数支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;百法明门论&gt; ，这是略录 &lt;瑜伽师地论、 本地分&gt; 中名数，以一切法无我为宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 粗释体义支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;大乘五蕴论&gt; ，这是摄 &lt;瑜伽师地论、 本地分&gt; 中境事，而以无我唯法为宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 总苞众义支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;显扬圣教论&gt; ，这是错综 &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 十七地要义，而以明教为宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 广苞大义支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;摄大乘论&gt; ，这是总括瑜伽、深密法门，诠释 &lt;阿毗达磨集论&gt;、 &lt;摄大乘论&gt; 宗要，以简小入地为宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、 分别名数支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;阿毗达磨杂集论&gt; ，这是总括 &lt;瑜伽师地论&gt; 一切法门，集 &lt;阿毗达磨经&gt; 所有宗要，以蕴、处、界三科为宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">六、 离僻彰中支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;辨中边论&gt; ，这是叙七品以成瑜伽法相，以中道为宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">七、 摧破邪山支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;二十唯识论&gt; ，这是释七难以成瑜伽唯识，以唯识无境为宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">八、 高建法幢支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;三十唯识论&gt;， 这是广诠瑜伽境体，以识外无别实有为宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">九、 庄严体义支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;大乘庄严论&gt; ，这是总括瑜伽菩萨一地法门，以庄严大乘为宗。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">十、 摄散归观支<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;分别瑜伽论&gt; ，此论中土未译。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a02"></a><span style="color:#333399">第二讲<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>三十颂科判大纲</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&lt;唯识三十颂&gt; ，是建立唯识宗的基本论典，古今注释三十颂的书不胜计数。在我国、以 &lt;成唯识论&gt; 最为重要。但 &lt;识论&gt; 十卷雄文，一方面是字字珠几，是发掘唯识要义的宝藏；另一方面它行文有如枝上岔枝，叶旁长叶。所谓 ‘文如钩锁，义若连环。’使人初读之下，如随入五里雾中，不知所来，亦不知所往。如何读通 ，成唯识论。 呢？唯有熟读本颂，以颂文对照识论，便有脉络可寻了。现在科分三十颂如下。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">一、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>三十颂科分</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三十颂，乃世亲菩萨所造，以五言四句为一颂，全文三十颂，计六百字。在一般经论中，多以三科分判，即序分、正宗分、流通分。而本颂全文皆是正宗分，并无序分和流通分。在讲解三十颂之前，先要熟读三十颂全文，全文即是：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">由假说我法<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>有种种相转<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>彼依识所变<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>此能变唯三</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">谓异熟思量<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>及了别境识<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>初阿赖耶识<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>异熟一切种</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">不可知执受<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>处了常与触<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>作意受想思<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>相应唯舍受</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">是无覆无记<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>触等亦如是<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>恒转如瀑流<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>阿罗汉位舍</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">次第二能变<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>是识名末那<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>依彼转缘彼<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>思量为性相</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">四烦恼常俱<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>谓我痴我见<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>并我慢我爱<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>及余触等俱</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">有覆无记摄<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>随所生所系<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>阿罗汉灭定<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>出世道无有</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">次第三能变<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>差别有六种<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>了境为性相<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>善不善俱非</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">此心所遍行<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>别境善烦恼<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>随烦恼不定<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>皆三受相应</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">初遍行触等<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>次别境谓欲<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>胜解念定慧<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>所缘事不同</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">善谓信惭愧<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>无贪等三根<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>勤安不放逸<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>行舍及不害</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">烦恼谓贪嗔<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>痴慢疑恶见<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>随烦恼谓忿<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>恨覆恼嫉悭</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">诳谄与害憍<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>无惭及无愧<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>掉举与昏沉<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>不信并懈怠</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">放逸及失念<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>散乱不正知<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>不定谓悔眠<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>寻伺二各二</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">依止根本识<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>五识随缘现<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>或俱或不俱<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>如波涛依水</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">意识常现起<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>除生无想天<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>及无心二定<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>睡眠与闷绝</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">是诸识转变<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>分别所分别<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>由此彼皆无<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>故一切唯识</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">由一切种识<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>如是如是变<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>以展转力故<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>彼彼分别生</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">由诸业习气<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>二取习气俱<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>前异熟既尽<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>复生余异熟</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">由彼彼遍计<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>遍计种种物<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>此遍计所执<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>自性无所有</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">依他起自性<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>分别缘所生<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>圆成实于彼<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>常远离前性</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">故此与依他<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>非异非不异<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>如无常等性<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>非不见此彼</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">即依此三性<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>立彼三无性<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>故佛密意说<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>一切法无性</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">初即相无性<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>次无自然性<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>后由远离前<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>所执我法性</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">此诸法胜义<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>亦即是真如<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>常如其性故<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>即唯识实性</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">乃至未起识<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>求住唯识性<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>于二取随眠<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>犹未能伏灭</span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">现前立少物<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>谓是唯识性<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>以有所得故<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>非实住唯识</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">若时于所缘<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>智都无所得<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>尔时住唯识<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>离二取相故</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">无得不思议<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>是出世间智<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>舍二粗重故<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>便证得转依</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><b><span style="color:teal">此即无漏界<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>不思议善常<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>安乐解脱身<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>大牟尼名法</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:teal"></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三十颂颂文，如上所录。本颂内容，以一切法唯识所现。即以识有非空，境无非有为宗。先破小乘外道，继明唯识之理。以文科判 有三种判别方法<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 以相、性、位三分科判<span lang="EN-US">： 即一者明唯识相； 二者明唯识性； 三者明唯位。这在三十首颂文中，由第一至第二十四颂是明唯识相，第二十五颂是明唯识性； 第二十六至第三十是明唯识位。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 以初、中、后三分科判<span lang="EN-US">： 在三十首颂文中，初一颂半为初分，次二十三颂半为中分，后五颂为后分。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 以境、行、果三分科判<span lang="EN-US">： 初二十五颂是明‘唯识境’，次四颂是明‘唯识行’，最后一颂是明‘唯识果’。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">现依第一种科判，分别说明三分如下<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 明唯识相<span lang="EN-US">： 即依他起性之法。依他起法，仗因托缘生起，唯识所现。凡夫外道，不知唯识无境之理，执心外有别实境，因此生起我执法执。故论主最初以种种方便，广明唯识相状、即是依他起之诸法，以破除其我执法执。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 明唯识性<span lang="EN-US">： 此即圆成实性，修唯识行者，虽知万法皆此心虚妄显现，而犹未能了达真性，是以次明唯识实性、即圆成实性，以此显示真如常住一味。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 明唯识位<span lang="EN-US">： 三十颂的前二十五颂，说明唯识相、性，依他圆成，无非是说明依他如幻，使修唯识行者，断妄染执障，证到圆成真理，而成三身万德的佛果。然佛果功德，殊妙无边，非少修行可能证圆，必须历经资粮、加行、通达、修习、究竟五位，十住、十行、十回向、十地、妙觉四十一阶，历经三大阿僧祗劫，方能至三身万德之佛地，故次第三，明唯识位。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">二、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>三十颂科分表</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">现依相、性、境三科分，列表示明如下：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">唯识三十颂分科表：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 明唯识相：前二十四须颂。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">甲、 略标：<span lang="EN-US">1、释难破执。2、标宗归识。3、彰能变体。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">乙、 广释：<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、明能变相：异熟能变、 思量能变、 了境能变、</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、正辨唯识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、通释妨难：释违理难、 释违教难、</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 明唯识性：第二十五颂。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 明唯识位：第二十六颂至第三十颂。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">依据上列的分科，于此拟定出讲解的顺序及内容，即是：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 释难破执：由假说我法，有种种相转。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 标宗归识：彼依识所变。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 彰能变体：此能变唯三，谓异熟、思量，及了别境识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 异熟能变：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、三相门：初阿赖耶识，异熟一切种。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、所缘行相门：不可知；执受、处、了。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、心所相应门：常与触、作意、受、想、思相应。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、五受相应门：(相应) 唯舍受。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、三性分别门：是无覆无记。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">6、心所例同门：触等亦如是。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">7、因果譬喻门：恒转如瀑流。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">8、伏断位次门：阿罗汉位舍。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、 思量能变：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、举体出名门：次第二能变，是识名末那。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、所依门：依彼转。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、所缘门：缘彼。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、体性行相门：思量为性相。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、心所相应门：四烦恼常俱，谓我痴我见，并我慢我爱，及余触等俱。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">6、三性分别门：有覆无记摄。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">7、界系分别门：随所生所系。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">8、起灭分位门：阿罗汉灭定，出世道无有。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">六、 了境能变：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、能变差别门：次第三能变，差别有六种。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、自性行相门：了境为性相。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、三性分别门：善不善俱非。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、相应俱受门：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">甲、 列名六位：此心所遍行，别境善烦恼，随烦恼不定。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">乙、 受俱分别：皆三受相应。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">丙、 重明五位：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">遍行：初遍行触等。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">别境： 次别境谓欲，胜解念定慧，所缘事不同。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">善：善谓信惭愧，无贪等三根，勤安不放逸，行舍及不害。<span lang="EN-US"></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">烦恼：烦恼为贪嗔，痴慢疑恶见。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">随烦恼：随烦恼为忿，恨覆恼嫉懂，诳谄与害娇，无惭及无愧、掉举与昏沉<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>不信并懈怠，放逸及失念，散乱不正知、不定：不定谓悔、眠，寻、伺二各二。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、所依门：依止根本识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">6、俱不俱转门：五识随缘现，或俱或不俱，如涛波依水。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">7、起灭分位门：意识常现起，除生无想天，及无心二定，睡眠与闷绝。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">七、 正辨唯识：是诸识转变，分别所分别，由此彼皆无，故一切唯识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">八、 释违理难<span lang="EN-US">——</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、心法生起缘由：由一切种识，如是如是变，以辗转力故，彼彼分别生。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、有情相续缘由：由诸业习气，二取习气俱，前异熟既尽，复生余异熟。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">九、 释违教难：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、三种自性：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">正辨：遍计所执性：由彼彼遍计，遍计种种物，此遍计所执，自性无所有。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">依他起性：依他起自性， 分别缘所生。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">圆成实性：圆成实于彼，常远离前性。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">明不一不异：故此与依他，非异非不异，如无常等性。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">明依圆前后：非不见此彼。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、三种无性：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">总说：即依此三性<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>立彼三无性<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>故佛密意说<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>一切法无性</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">别明：相无性：初即相无性。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">生无性：次无自然性。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">胜义无性：后由远离前，所执我法性。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">十、 明唯识性：此诸法胜义，亦即是真如，常如其性故，即唯识实性。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">十一、 明唯识位：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、资粮位：乃至未起识，求住唯识性，于二取随眠，犹未能伏灭。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、加行位：现前立少物，谓是唯识性，以有所得故，非实住唯识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、通达位：若时于所缘，智都无所得，尔时住唯识，离二取相故。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、修习位：无得不思议，是出世间智，舍二粗重故，便证得转依。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、究竟位：此即无漏界，不思议善常，安乐解脱身，大牟尼名法。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">三、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>与三十颂相关的论典</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">讲完三十科判大纲，再介绍几本与三十颂相关的论典。首先要介绍的是注释三十颂的<span lang="EN-US">&lt;成唯识论&gt; ，凡十卷，护法等十大论师各造释论，唐代玄奘三藏奉诏译，翻经沙门窥基笔受，这是学习唯识学必读的重要论书。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">世亲晚年造<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;唯识三十颂&gt; ，本颂造出，未造释文而入寂，未几十大论师继起，各造释论，斯时法海波澜，至为壮阔。唐代玄奘三藏由印度回国，携回十家释论百卷，奘师译此论时，本主张十家释论各别全译，后以弟子窥基之请，糅集十家之义成为一部，其中异义纷纭之处，悉折中于护法之说，故 &lt;成唯识论&gt; 十卷，虽说是糅集十师之作，而实以护法一家为宗，名为传译，不啻新造。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">基师亦尝述其传译参糅之绩云<span lang="EN-US">： 十家别译之初，神[日＋方]、嘉尚、普光、窥基四人同受师命，共同翻译。数日之后，基请退出，奘师固问其故，基对曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[群圣制作，各驰誉于五天，虽文具传于贝叶，而义不备于一本，情见各异，禀者无依。请错综群言，以为一本，楷定真谬，权衡盛则。’ 久之奘师乃许，故得此论行世。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">其次介绍<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;成唯识论述记&gt; ，述记十卷 (或二十卷，亦有六十卷本) ，是唐代大成法相唯识宗的窥基大师撰述，这是注解 &lt;成唯识论&gt; 的著作。本书内容分为五门，即：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 教时机，分为说教时会与教所被机两种。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 论宗体<span lang="EN-US">： 以唯识为宗而谓其体有四重。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 藏乘所摄<span lang="EN-US">： 谓 &lt;成唯识论&gt; 为一乘之所摄，并为三藏中之菩萨乘所摄。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 说教年主<span lang="EN-US">： 以慧恺之 &lt;俱舍论&gt; 序论说世亲与十大论师之年代。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、 本文判释<span lang="EN-US">： 即就本文述释其义。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">述记一书，是窥基随奘师笔受<span lang="EN-US">‘识论’时，以所闻之于师者，随时笔劄，识论完成，更为此记。凡识论中不尽之义，及己意当发抒者，皆于此记中见之。但这相当于随堂笔记，素称难读。传说清末状元夏同和，初读 ‘识论’，谓有如月下看花，再读述记，如堕如五里雾中。故学者若不专业研究，莫不半途而废，不能竟卷也。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">本书元代即告失传，清代末年杨仁山居士得之于日本，由金陵刻经处刻印行世。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&lt;成唯识论掌中枢要&gt; 四卷，也是窥基撰述，略称 &lt;成唯识论枢要&gt; ，系唯识三疏之一。本书初叙 &lt;成唯识论&gt; 之成立、传入、揉译等因缘，次释本论之题目及所被之根机。再次释论文，于识论述记之未详尽处，更详加解释。其中对于唯识三十颂科判、五种姓、三类境等问题，均广泛加以解释。收入大正藏四十三册。注释书有唐外智周撰 &lt;成唯识论枢要记&gt; 二卷，唐代憬兴之 &lt;成唯识论枢要记&gt; 二卷。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&lt;成唯识论了义灯&gt; 七卷 (或十三卷) ，是窥基的弟子慧沼撰述，略称 &lt;唯识了义灯&gt; ，唯识三疏之一。本书系显慈恩宗正义，而破斥有关解释 &lt;成唯识论&gt; 中的异说者。事实上是祖述窥基之说，而责难圆测、圆义、普光、慧观等之异说。此书颇有门户之见，且素称不易解读。本书收入大正藏第四十三册。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&lt;成唯识论演秘&gt;<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>七卷 (或十四卷) ，是慧沼的弟子智周所撰，略称 &lt;识论演秘&gt; ，是注解 &lt;成唯识论&gt; 及 &lt;成唯识论述记&gt; 之书，亦为唯识三疏之一。现收入大正藏第四十三册。所谓‘唯识三疏’，是注释 &lt;成唯识论&gt; 、及 &lt;成唯识论述记&gt; 的三种注疏，即窥基撰的 &lt;成唯识论掌中枢要&gt; ，慧沼撰的 &lt;成唯识论了义灯&gt; ，及智周撰的 &lt;成唯识论演秘&gt; 。而注释‘述记’的书，有唐代道邑之 &lt;成唯识论义蕴&gt; 五卷，如理之 &lt;成唯识论疏义演&gt; 二十六卷，灵泰之 &lt;成唯识论疏钞&gt; 十八卷等。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
