<p style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">三、平等性智相应位：菩萨见道位、修道位、法空智果现前，及转识成智，证得佛果，均此位所摄。</p>
<p style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt">以上三位，前二位是有漏位，第三位是无漏位。在有漏二位中，第一位是染污位，第二位是不染污位。</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a07"></a><span style="color:#333399">第七讲<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>了境能变——第六识</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三能变识的第三能，是了别境能变。了别境能变指前六识而言，故三十颂颂文称<span lang="EN-US">‘次第三能变<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>差别有六种。’根据 &lt;成唯识论&gt; 的科判，以七段九义来解释颂文，现列其科判如下：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">┌</span><span lang="EN-US">1</span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、能变差别门————次第三能变，差别有六种———体别门</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US">2</span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、自性行相门————了境为性——————————自性门</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">相——————————行相门</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US">3</span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、三性分别门————善不善俱非—————————三性门</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US">4</span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、相应门：</span><span lang="EN-US"> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>A</span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、列六位—此心所遍行，别境善烦恼，随烦恼不定—相应门</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>B</span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、受俱——皆三受相应—————————————受俱门</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">┌遍行——初遍行触等</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│别境——次别境为欲，胜解念定慧</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">七段┤</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│善———善谓信惭愧，无贪等三根</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">九义│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">释│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">勤安不放逸，行舍及不害</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span> <span lang="EN-US">C</span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、六┤烦恼——烦恼为贪嗔，痴慢疑恶见</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">位│随烦恼—随烦恼为忿，恨覆恼嫉懂</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">诳谄与害娇，无惭及无愧</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">掉举与昏沉，不信并懈怠</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">放逸及失念，散乱不正如</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">└不定——不定谓悔眠，寻伺二各二</span><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US">5</span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、所依门—依止根本识——————————————所依门</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">│</span><span lang="EN-US">6</span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、俱转不俱转门—————————————————俱转门</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:42.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:3.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">└</span><span lang="EN-US">7</span><span style="font-family:细明体;mso-ascii-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">、起灭分位门——————————————————起灭门</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">一、 能变差别门<span lang="EN-US">—— 次第三能变<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>差别有六种</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[次第三能变’ ，是对初之异熟能变，次之思量能变而言，现在是第三了境能变。‘差别有六种’句，谓了别境识是前六识的总名，若分别来说，包括眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意六种识，了别色、声、香、味、触、法六种境。这六识得名的由来，有随根得名和随境得名两种。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 随根立名<span lang="EN-US">： 随所依之根，而立六识之命。即依于眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意六根，，而立眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意六识之名，</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 随境立名<span lang="EN-US">： 即是随其所缘之境，而立六识之名。前六识所缘之境，是色、声、香、味、触、法六境，以其了别的尘境，而立色、声、香、味、触、法六识之名。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">唯随根立名通于自在位<span lang="EN-US"> (八地以上菩萨，可以五根互用) ，随境立名不通于自在位，故论典中多从随根立名。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">这六种识，前五识是五种感觉器官，依于眼、耳、鼻、舌、身五根，而生出的五种认识作用。第六识依于意根，是心理活动的综合中心。这六识的作用是<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 眼识<span lang="EN-US">： 依于眼根，缘色境而生起了别认识作用</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 耳识<span lang="EN-US">： 依于耳根，缘声境而生起了别认识作用。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 鼻识<span lang="EN-US">： 依于鼻根，缘香境而生起了别认识作用。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 舌识<span lang="EN-US">： 依于舌根，缘味境而生起了别认识作用。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、 身识<span lang="EN-US">： 依于身根，缘触境而生起了别认识作用。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">六、 意识：依于意根，缘法境而生起了别认识作用。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">意识与前五识任何一识俱起，同缘外境，发生了别作用时，顺次生起的五种心念<span lang="EN-US">，即：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 率尔心<span lang="EN-US">： 意识初对外境，于刹那间的轻率了别。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 寻求心<span lang="EN-US">： 于率尔了别之后，进而生起寻求作用。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 决定心<span lang="EN-US">： 意识寻到目标，进而决心了别。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 染净心<span lang="EN-US">： 意识于了别外境后，对于怨亲顺违等境界，所生起的染净之心。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、 等流心<span lang="EN-US">： 染净之心 (善恶之心) 相续，即叫做等流心。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">以上五心，顺次生起，而前五识之染净，必定由意识为之引导。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">第六识的作用有两方面，一者意识与前五识同时而起，发生其了别作用，曰五俱意识；二者意识不与前五识同时俱起，而单独生起，称为独头意识，分释如下：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 五俱意识：意识与前五识俱起，共同了别境。五俱不是同时五俱，而是或一俱，或二俱，或三、或五俱，视缘而定。即<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、意识与眼识同起，发生其分别作用，称眼俱意识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、意识与耳识同起，发生其分别作用，称耳俱意识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、意识与鼻识同起，发生其分别作用，称鼻俱意识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、意识与舌识同起，发生其分别作用，称舌俱意识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、意识与身识同起，发生其分别作用，称身俱意识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 独头意识：又称独散意识，即不与前五识俱起，而单独发生作用，此复有四种：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、独散意识：或追忆过去，或筹计未来，或比较推度种种想像分别，或意念游走东想西想，此称独散意识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、梦中独头意识：这是在睡梦中，缘梦中境界而生起的意识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、定中独头意识：这是在禅定中，缘定中境界所生起的意识。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、狂乱独头意识：狂是颠狂，类以精神病患者，他独言独语，或辅以肢体动作，别人不知所以，事实上他的意识、也是缘著他自己幻想的境界而活动。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">二、 自性行相门<span lang="EN-US">——了境为性相</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">前六识皆以了别境界为其自性，也为其行相，所以说<span lang="EN-US">‘了境为性相]。 颂文中‘了境为’三字应重读，即了境为性，了境为相。性者体性，指识体的自证分；相者行相，即是作用，指能缘的见分。本来了别外境只是前六识的行相，以其体性微细难知，故以用显体，故双云了境为相，了境为性。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">三、 三性分别门<span lang="EN-US">——善不善俱非</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[善不善俱非]一句，不是说前五识非善非不善，而是说此六个识，通于善、恶、无记三性。此六识生起，与十一个善心所相应者，就是善； 与二十六个烦恼心所相应者，就是恶； 与善或烦恼心所均不相应者，就是无记。本来前五识只是感觉器官，没有善恶的分别，但以第六识的五俱意识与之俱起，五俱意识随著前五识缘境而了解分别，这时前五识随著第六识的引导，亦就通于三性了。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">四、 相应门<span lang="EN-US">——六位心所 (颂文不俱录)</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">相应门，指与了别境能变识的相应心所而言。相应二字，有<span lang="EN-US">‘合作’的意义。它建立在时、依、缘、事的四义上。至于‘心所’二字，是心所有法的略称， &lt;成唯识论&gt; 曰：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[恒依心起，与心相应，系属于心，故名心所。’ 分释三义如下：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 恒依心起<span lang="EN-US">： 心王生起时，心所同时俱起，心王若无时，心所亦不生，它是依于心王势力方得生起。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 与心相应<span lang="EN-US">： 心所依心王生起，复与心王协合如一，名为相应。相应复有五义：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、所依同： 心王与心所同依于一根，方得相应。如眼识心所，与眼识心王同依于一眼根。耳、鼻、舌、身等亦然。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、所缘同： 心所与心王俱缘一境，曰所缘同。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、行相相似： 心王心所各自有其固有的性能，但以‘相似’故，如眼识心王心所同缘青色时，王、所之相分即各别变作青色之相分。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、时同： 王、所俱时而生，无有先后。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、事同： 事字在此处是 ‘体’义，于一聚相应心王心所中，如心王自体是一，心所亦各各是一，如眼识一聚相应的心王心所，眼识心王是一，则触、作意等心所其体亦各各是一，例同心王。事实上，亦绝无一法，于一时中有二体并转者。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 系属于心<span lang="EN-US">： 以心王为主，心所系属之，心王有自在力，为心所之所依。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">在百法中，心所有五十一个，分为六位，即遍行心所五，别境心所五，善心所十一，烦恼心所六，随烦恼心所二十，不定心所六，现在分别诠释如下<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 遍行心所<span lang="EN-US">： 六位心所的第一位，共有五个，即颂文：‘初遍行触等’，触以下是作意、受、想、思。此已见于第五讲异熟能变识中，此处不赘。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 别境心所<span lang="EN-US">： 六位心所的第二位，共有五个，即颂文：‘次别境谓欲，胜解、念、定、慧，所缘事不同。’所谓别境，以此五心所所缘之境，各别不同，非如遍行同缘一境。欲所缘者为所乐境，胜解所缘者为决定境，念所缘者为曾所习境，定所缘者为所观境，慧则于四境拣择为性。此五种心所，乃必作之心，善恶皆然。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">此五心所，具一切性<span lang="EN-US">——善恶无记； 一切地——三界九地，而不缘一切境，亦非相续。非心有即有，故无一切时； 非与一切心相应，故无一切俱。兹分述如下：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、欲心所：欲是希望， &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[于所缘境，希望为性，勤依为业。’ 故欲的自性就是希望，于所爱境希望必合，于所恶境希望必离。‘勤依为业’者，因为希望，方勤劬精进，故欲为勤之所依，能为勤所依，即是其业用。唯所谓精进，系指对善欲而言，若不善欲，就不是精进了。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、胜解心所：胜者殊胜，解者见解，即是殊胜的见解。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[于决定境，印持为性，不可引转为业。’ 所谓决定境，即于所缘实境、或义理境，无所犹豫。如缘青色，计此为青，不疑为红为蓝； 如受某种学说影响，对其义理承受无疑，均名决定境。心识于缘虑决定境时，有审决印持的作用，此即胜解的自性。既经审决印可，即不可引转，即其业用。于犹豫境，则不起胜解。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、念心所：念是记忆，于所经历过的事物记忆不忘，就称为念。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[于曾习境，令心明记，不忘为性，定依为业。’ 凡是感官接触过的境界，或思维过的义理，都是曾习境，于曾习境的记忆作用，就是念的自性； 定依为业者，由忆念曾习正理，念兹在兹，而生正定，即是其业用。但于未曾经历的境是，则不起忆念。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、定心所：定的梵语三摩地，译曰正定， &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[于所观境，令心专注，不散为性，智依为业。’ 令心专注是心力恒时凝聚，不随所缘流散，故心力专注是其自性，由心定之故，明智即生，此即其业用。散乱之心，不能生定，亦无所依之智。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、慧心所：慧即智慧，是明白拣择， &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>&lt;于所观境，简择为性，断疑为业。’ 简择是比量智，于一切所知境界，简择其得失，而推度决定，故简择即慧之自性，由拣择而除掉疑惑，即是慧的业用。在愚昧心中，疑惑心中，则不能起慧。再者，邪见之流，以其痴增上故，不能简择，亦不起慧。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 善心所：六位心所的第三位，计有十一个，即信、惭、愧、无贪、无嗔、无痴、精进、轻安、不放逸、行舍、不害。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">何谓善，随顺法理，于此世他世顺益于自他者，谓之善<span lang="EN-US">； 反之，于此世他世损害于自他者，名不善。故以上十一种善心所，赅括世出世间一切善法，其自体远离一切秽恶，而聚集一切功德。兹分述如下：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、信心所：信是对佛教义理坚定的信仰。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为信，于实德能深忍乐欲，心净为性，对治不信乐善为业。’ 信有三种，一者于诸法实事实理深信不疑； 二者于三宝净德深为信乐； 三者于一切善法深信有力，能得成就。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、惭心所：惭者羞恶之心，是自我人格的尊重，做了坏事内心感到羞耻，曰惭。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为惭依自法力，崇重贤善为性，对治无惭，止息恶行为业。]由于本身自我尊重的促进之力，可以止息恶行。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、愧心所：愧者廉耻之心，尊重世间舆论，耻于自己过失。即做了坏事无颜见人曰愧。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为愧，依世间力，轻拒暴恶为性，对治无愧，止息恶行为业。’ 愧和惭一样，可以止息恶行。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、无贪心所：对于财色名利无贪著之心曰无贪。&lt;识论&gt;<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>曰：<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何无贪，于有有具无著为性，对治贪著作善为业。’有是三有之果，三有即欲界、色界、无色界三界，这是有情生存的处所； 有具，是生于三有的原因，即是惑与业。无贪是对有情生存处所不生贪著，不造惑业。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、无嗔心所：逆境当前，不生恚恨之心，谓之无嗔。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何无嗔，于苦苦具，无恚为性，对治嗔恚，作善为业。’ 苦是三界苦果，即三苦——苦苦、坏苦、行苦。苦具，即生苦之因。对于苦及生苦之因，不起嗔恚之心，于诸有情，常存慈愍，曰无嗔。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">6、无痴心所：无痴，是明达事理，不为迷惑。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何无痴，于诸理事明解为性，对治愚痴，作善为业。’ 所谓明解理事，是指明确理解四圣谛、八正道等佛教义理而言。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">7、精进心所：此又名勤，即对修道、为善勤劬不懈。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[勤为精进，于善恶品，修断事中，勇悍为性，对治懈怠，满善为业。’ 精者不杂，进者不退；勇而无惰，悍而无惧。精进是修善断恶，勤于为恶者正是颠倒，不名精进。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">8、轻安心所：身心安适轻快，谓之轻安。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[安谓轻安，远离粗重，调畅身心，堪任为性，对治昏沉，转依为业。’ 粗重指贪痴烦恼而言，修行者调伏烦恼，远离粗重，为修禅定之必要条件。转依为业者，即转去粗重，依于轻安。此心所唯于定中生起。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">9、不放逸心所：对治放逸，断恶修善，曰不放逸。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[不放逸者，精进三根，依所修断，防修为怍，对治放逸，成满一切世出世间善业。’ 放逸是在贪、嗔、痴的基础上成就一切恶事； 不放逸，是在无贪无嗔无痴的基础上成就一切善事。精进三根，指精进、无贪、无嗔、无痴四法，不放逸是四法分位假立之法，别无实体。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">10、 行舍心所：行者行蕴，舍即舍弃，贪嗔痴三法令心昏沉掉举，舍弃昏沉、掉举，令心得到平等，安于寂静。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何行舍，精进三根，令心平等正直，无功用住为性，对治掉举，静住为业。’ 此亦精进三根上分位假立之法。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">11、 不害心所：不害即不恼损众生，以无嗔为性，于诸有情，不为恼损。 &lt;识论&gt;曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何不害，于诸有情不为恼损，无嗔为性，能对治害，悲愍为业。’ 不害是损恼有情之害的反面，无嗔是慈，予众生以乐； 不害是悲，拔众生以苦。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a08"></a><span style="color:#333399">第八讲<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>前六识的王所相应至起灭分位</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">本讲上次讲到相应门<span lang="EN-US">——即与前六识相应的心所，以课文过长，未能讲完，现在继续上一讲再往下讲解。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 烦恼心所：六位心所的第四位，计有贪、嗔、痴、慢、疑、恶见六种。此又称六种根本烦恼，由此能生起随之而来的随烦恼。<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[烦恼心所，其相云何，颂曰： 烦恼谓贪嗔，痴慢疑恶见。论曰： 此贪等六，性是根本烦恼摄故，得烦恼名。’何谓烦恼，烦者烦闷、烦扰，恼者恼乱、恼热， &lt;大智度论&gt; 七曰：[烦恼者，能令心烦，能作恼故，名为烦恼。’ 兹分述如下：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、贪心所：贪即贪欲， &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为贪，于有、有具染著为性，能障无贪，生苦为业。’ 有即三有或三界，有具是生起三有之因，也就是惑与业。贪以染著为性，著即执著，执著于我及我所，对于财色杖位固持不释，障蔽无贪之心，起惑造业，堕于三有，承受苦报。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、嗔心所：嗔者嗔恚，与无嗔反。&lt;识论&gt; 曰：‘云何为嗔，于苦、苦具，憎恚为性，能障无嗔，不安隐性，恶行所依为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">苦即三苦<span lang="EN-US">——苦苦、坏苦、行苦，苦具是造成三苦之因。嗔是对三苦及造成三苦之因生恚恨心，能令身心恼热，对家人眷属，一切众生，轻则诟骂，重则损害他命，甚至于伐城伐国，喋血千里，莫不由嗔心而起。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、痴心所：痴是愚昧不明，事理颠倒，因果迷乱，义理全乖，是无痴之反。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰 ：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为痴，于诸理事，迷□为性，能障无痴，一切杂染所依为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">痴即十二缘起之首的无明，无明即是迷昧不觉，对世间道理及佛法义理迷惑不解，由此引起种种烦恼，即<span lang="EN-US">‘一切杂染所依为业’。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、慢心所：慢者傲慢，自以为处处优于他人。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为慢，恃已于他，高举为性，能障不慢，生苦为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">慢者自尊自大，轻举乔扬，不知谦卑，轻蔑他人。<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;俱舍论&gt; 把慢区分为七或九种，唯识宗继承了‘七慢’之说条。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">A、慢： 对于不如我的，我轻慢他，这叫 ‘于劣计己胜’； 对于和我相等者，我轻慢他，这叫‘于等计己等’。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">B、过慢： 对方和我相等，我以为胜过他，这叫 ‘于等计己胜’； 对方胜过我，我不承认，反说我胜过他，这叫‘于胜计己胜’。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">C、过过慢： 对方胜过我，我不承认，反说我胜过他甚多，这叫做 ‘于胜计己胜]。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">D、我慢： 执著于五蕴和合的身心，为我与我所，因而骄傲自大，叫做我慢。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">E、增上慢： 修行者 ‘未得言得，未证言证。’叫做增上慢。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">F、卑劣慢： 自甘卑劣的人，对于胜过他的人，以为 ：‘胜过我又该如何？ ’别人学佛修道，他以为：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[我不信佛，还不是照样过日子？ ’此为自甘卑劣之慢。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">G、邪慢： 于慢上起邪见，自己无德，反说：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[佛菩萨也不过如此’。甚至于不信因果，毁谤三宝，这叫邪慢。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、疑心所：对真理怀疑不定，曰疑。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为疑，于诸谛理，犹豫为性，能障不疑善品为业。’ 所谓谛理，即苦、集、灭、道四圣谛而言。对谛理犹豫不信，故障蔽不疑的善品，此即其业用。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">6、恶见心所：恶见又称不正见，亦即是邪见。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何恶见，于诸谛理，颠倒推求，染慧为性，能障善见，招苦为业。’ 恶见心所是依慧心所所假立的，故云以为性。而慧通于善、恶、无记三性，此慧是染分之慧，非善性所摄，染慧能障善见，招感苦果，故称招苦为业。恶见可开为五种，即：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">A、萨伽耶见： 译曰身见，这是一种外道的见解，认为五蕴实有，执此为我，而生种种谬误的见解。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[萨伽耶见，谓于五取蕴执我我所，一切见趣所依为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">B、边见： 有了我见，即计度我为死后常住不灭者，或计度我为死断灭者，此即佛教所反对的常见或断见。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">C、邪见： 认为世间无生果之因，亦无可招之果，故为恶不足惧，为善不足法，此种见解，乃见之最邪者，故名邪见。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">D、见取见： 于前种见上随执一端，以为最胜，即固执其所见，一切斗争依之而起，故以一切斗争所依为业。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">E、戒禁取见： 印度古代苦行外道，认为受持牛、狗、鸡等戒，可以得涅槃之果。这种非因计因，非道计道之见，是为戒禁取见。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、 随烦恼心所：六位心所的第五位，此又名随惑，是随根本烦恼所生起的烦恼。随有三义，一者自类俱起，二者遍不善性，三者遍诸染心。随烦恼心所二十个，分为小随、中随、大随三种。小随烦恼十个、中随烦恼二十个、大随烦恼八个。小、中、大的分别，以三义俱备者名大随，兼具二义者称中随<span lang="EN-US"> (自类俱起、遍不善性) 。于不善心中各别而起者称小随。现分述如下：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">小随烦恼心所，随根本烦恼生起之烦恼，计有十种，曰忿、恨、覆、恼、嫉、悭、诳、谄、害、乔。其发生作用面最小，而行相粗猛，于不善心中，各别生起。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">中随烦恼，随根本烦恼生起之烦恼，有二种，曰无惭、无愧，其发生之作用范围较小随烦恼为宽，俱自类俱起，遍不善心二义，故曰中随。此二者，对自己所犯的过恶不感到羞耻，是其共同点<span lang="EN-US">； 而惭者‘轻拒贤善’，愧者‘崇重暴恶’，是其相异点。大随烦恼，随根本烦恼生起之烦恼，有八种，曰掉举、昏沉、不信、懈怠、放逸、失念、散乱、不正知，其发生作用范围最广，俱自类俱起，遍不善性，遍诸染心三义，故曰大随烦恼。现分述二十种随烦恼如下：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、忿心所：对于违逆之境生起的忿怒，产生粗暴的身语表业。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为忿，依对现前不饶益境，愤发为性，能障不愤，执杖为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、恨心所：恨者怨恨，怀恶不舍，引起极度烦恼。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为恨，由忿为先，怀恶不舍，结怨为性，能障不恨，热恼为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、覆心所：覆是覆盖，犯了过恶，怕丧失名利，故把过恶隐藏起来。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：[云何为覆，于自罪恶，恐失利誉，隐藏为性，能障不覆，悔恼为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、恼心所：恼者恼怒，于忿恨之后，遇违逆事，因而爆怒，凶狠暴戾，有如蝎子螫人。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为恼，忿恨为先，追触暴热，狠戾为性，能障不恼，蛆螫为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、嫉心所：嫉者妒忌，他人荣盛，我怀忧戚，如妾妇之固宠，政敌之倾轧。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰 ：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为嫉，殉自名利，不耐他荣，妒忌为性，能障不嫉，忧戚为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">6、悭心所：悭者悭吝，财物不肯施舍，法理秘不告人，鄙恶地蓄积财法。 &lt;识论&gt;曰：‘云何为悭，耽著财法，不能惠施，秘吝为性，能障不悭，鄙蓄为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">7、诳心所：诳是欲谋取名誉或利益，自己无德而诈称有德的一种欺骗行为。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰 ：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为诳，为获利誉，矫现有德，诡诈为性，能障不诳，邪命为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">8、谄心所：谄者谄曲，为了取得别人欢心而阿谀谄媚，以达到自己谋求的目的。 &lt;识论 &gt; 曰：‘云何为谄，为冈他故，矫设导仪，险曲为性，能障不谄，教诲为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">9、害心所：害者损害，心无悲愍，损害有情，是不害之反。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为害，于诸有情，心无悲愍，损恼为性，能障不害，逼恼为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">10、 乔心所：乔者骄傲，由于得到世间名利而骄慢自大。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何为乔，于自盛事，深生染著，醉傲为性，能障不乔，染依为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">11、 无惭心所：无惭是惭之反，即没有羞恶之心，不顾本身人格尊严，拒绝贤人的教诲，不接受世间出世间善法。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何无惭，不顾自法，轻拒贤善为性，能障碍惭，生长恶行为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">12、 无愧心所：无愧是愧之反，没有廉耻之心，不顾世间清议，不畏社会舆论。 &lt;识论&gt;曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何无愧，不顾世间，崇重暴恶为性，能障碍愧，生长恶行为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">13、 掉举心所：掉举是心不安静，妄动浮燥，障碍禅定。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何掉举，令心于境不寂静为性，能障行舍奢摩他为业。’ 奢摩他为‘止’，即是禅定。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">14、 昏沉心所：昏沉是昏懵沉醉，迷□不明，障碍轻安和智慧。 &lt;识论&gt;<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>曰：‘云何昏沉，令心于境无堪任为性，能障轻安毗钵舍那为业。’ 毗钵舍那是‘观]，与奢摩他合称‘止观’。此又称定慧、寂照。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">15、 不信心所：不信者心存污秽，不信三相，即一者实有，即诸法实相； 二者德，即佛、法、僧三宝； 三者有能，有能力成就世出世间善法。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何不信，于实、德、能不忍乐欲，心秽为性，能障净信，堕依为业，谓不信者多懈怠故。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">16、 懈怠心所：懈怠与精进相反，既不修善，亦不断恶，甚而对恶业勤奋。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何懈怠，于善恶品修断事中，懒堕为性，能障精进，增染为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">17、 放逸心所：放逸者，放荡纵逸，于染法不能防，于净法不肯修。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：[云何放逸，于染净品不能防修，纵荡为性，障不放逸，增恶损善所依为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">18、 失念心所：失念即是遗忘，心意散乱，对于所修善法不能明记。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：[云何失念，于诸所缘，不能明记为性，能障正念，散乱所依为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">19、 散乱心所：散乱即不专心，令心流荡，，障碍正定，阻止善慧，增长恶慧。 &lt;识论&gt;曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何散乱，于诸所缘，令心流荡为性，能障正定，恶慧所依为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">20、 不正知心所：不正知即是邪知，误解世间法及出世间法，破坏佛教真理。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰 ：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[云何不正知，于所观境，谬解为性，能障正知，毁犯为业。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">六、 不定心所：六位心所的第六位，有四种，曰悔、眠、寻、伺。称不定者，意谓于识、性<span lang="EN-US"> (善、恶、无记。) 界 (欲、色、无色三界。) 都不确定。无法记别。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、悔心所：又名恶作，对于先所作事生起悔心。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[悔谓恶作，恶所作业，追悔为性，障止为业。’ 即对已作恶事追悔，就是善性； 对已作善事追悔，就是恶性。悔能令心怅怏不安，故有障碍止 (观) 作用。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、眠心所：眠即睡眠，昏迷而不自在，能障智慧。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[眠谓睡眠，令身不自在，昧略为性，障观为业。’ 睡眠之时，心极阇劣，身无力用，故有障碍 (止) 观的作用。故适度睡眠是为善法，过度睡眠是为恶法。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、寻心所：寻者寻求，对事理粗略具思考。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[寻谓寻求，令心偬遽，于意言境，粗转为性。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、伺心所：伺者伺察，对事理细密的思考。 &lt;识论&gt; 曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[何谓伺察，令心偬遽，于意言境，细转为性。’ 寻与伺，是依思心所与慧心所分位假立，本身没有实体。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">五、 所依门<span lang="EN-US">——依止根本识</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">第三能变识，是集合前五识与第六识所合成，此六识之生起，皆以第八识为依止，故颂文首句指出：<span lang="EN-US">‘依止根本识’。识论解释此句曰：‘根本识者，阿陀那识，染净诸识生根本故。依止者，谓前六转识，以根本识为共亲依。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">心、心所的生起，要有三种依，即因缘依，增上缘依，等无间缘依。而前六识之生起，以种子赖耶为亲因缘，得有前六识之现行。再者，前五识以五根为不共依，而五根由现行第八识执受得有，故前五识亦可说是以现行第八识为所依，这是根本共依。再者，第六识以第七识为所依，而第七识以现行第八识为不共依，所以第六识可以说是以第八识为根本共依。简单的说，<span lang="EN-US">‘依止根本识’者，即是前六识以现行赖耶为共依——增上缘依，而以种子赖耶为亲因缘依。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">增上缘依非现行赖耶一种，而是有四种，若缺任何一种，五识即不生起，此四种依为<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 同境依<span lang="EN-US">： 前五识依于眼耳鼻舌身五色根，此五根与五识共取现境，曰同境依。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 分别依<span lang="EN-US">： 谓依于第六识，前五识任何一识生起，意识与之同时生起，与前五识同缘色声等境，而起了解分别，曰分别依。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 染净依<span lang="EN-US">： 谓依于第七识，第七识与‘四烦恼常俱’，是染污识，前五识亦由此识染污而成有漏，故此第七识是前五识的染净依。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 根本依<span lang="EN-US">： 谓依于第八识，第八识是根本识，前五识依第八识而得生起，故以第八识为根本依。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">六、 俱不俱转门<span lang="EN-US">——五识随缘现<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>或俱或不俱<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>如涛波依水</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">颂文<span lang="EN-US"> ‘五识随缘’句，指前五识生起，必须众缘俱备，而五识俱缘各不相同，如眼识所缘的物件是色境，生起时需要九缘；而耳识需八缘，鼻舌身三识需七缘，兹分述如下：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 眼识九缘<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、空缘： 空即空间，眼识取境，须保持适当距离，无空间不能取境。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、明缘： 明即光明，眼识取境，需要光明，无光明不能取境。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">3、根缘： 眼识依于眼根而生起。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">4、境缘： 眼根触对色境而生眼识，境为识之所缘缘。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">5、作意缘： 作意即是注意，不注意则 ‘视而不见’。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">6、分别依缘： 分别指第六识，依第六识以分别外境。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">7、染净依缘： 此指第七识，对怨亲顺违之境生起的染净心。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">8、根本依缘： 此指第八识，第八识为前七识之根本。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">9、种子依： 种子为生起识之亲因缘。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 耳识八缘<span lang="EN-US">： 耳识生起，不需光明，故仅需八缘。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 鼻、舌、身三识，是<span lang="EN-US">‘合中取境’，不需光明和距离，故只需七缘。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">或俱或不俱者，五识可同时生起，亦可或一、或二、或三四生起，视缘而定。如波涛依水句，喻藏识如大海，余识如波涛，外境如风，风起而波涛现。<span lang="EN-US"> &lt;八识规矩颂&gt; 谓：‘浩浩三藏不可穷，渊深七浪境为风。’即指此而言。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">七、 起灭分位门<span lang="EN-US">——意识常现起，除生无想天，及无心二定，睡眠与闷绝。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">在上节俱不俱转门中，虽然统指第三能变识而言，实际上讲的只是前五识。此门则唯就第六识的起灭予以说明。前五识生起，须俱或九或八或七缘，俱缘较多，缘不俱足则有中断。第六识生起，只俱根缘、境缘、作意缘、根本依缘、种子依缘五种，缘少较易俱，故常时现起。但有五种情形则不生起，此称为<span lang="EN-US">[五位无心’。此五种情形是：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 生于无想天<span lang="EN-US">： 外道修行生于无想天，寿命五百大劫，在此期间意识不起现行。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 入无想定<span lang="EN-US">： 外道修行，入无想定，意识不起现行。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 灭尽定<span lang="EN-US">： 修此定者，前六识不起现行，第七识染心所亦不起现行。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 睡眠<span lang="EN-US">； 深度熟睡而无梦者，意识不起现行。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、 闷绝<span lang="EN-US">： 俗称昏迷，医学上谓‘无意识状态’，这是由于大惊布、大剌激，或剧痛昏晕的情况下，前六识不起现行。但第七、八识仍恒时相续，故闷绝者并非死亡，而是第六识不起现行。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><a name="a09"></a><span style="color:#333399">第九讲<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>正辨唯识与释违理难</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">以前八讲，由唯识学统，科判大纲，讲到唯识学的基本概念，以至于三能变识，三十颂颂文已讲完十六颂，今天讲十七、十八、十九等三颂。这三颂在科判中是：七、 正辨唯识，八、 释违理难。释违理难又分为两个子目，即心法生起缘由，及有情相续缘由，故分做三段来讲。现在即依诠释。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">一<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</span>正辨唯识——是诸识转变，分别所分别，由此彼皆无，故一切唯识。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">正辨唯识的颂文，如标题所录。这一首颂文，是上承首颂<span lang="EN-US">‘彼依识所变，此能变唯三’二句，以‘是诸识转变，分别所分别’二句，来说明万法唯识的道理；再以‘由此彼皆无，故一切唯识’二句，总结之于唯识。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">在三能变的颂文中，说明八识及各各心所，皆由自证分变现的见分和相分。但外人仍继续追问：<span lang="EN-US">‘如何能知道宇宙万有，皆是识所变现，而无实我实法的存在呢？’唯识家为了解答这一问题，复说下颂曰：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[是诸识转变，分别所分别，由此彼皆无，故一切唯识。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&lt;成唯识论&gt; 解释此颂曰：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[是诸识者，谓前所说，三能变识，及彼心所，皆能变似见相二分，立转变名。所变见分，说名分别，能取相故。所变相分，名所分别，见所取故。由此正理，彼实我法，离识所变，定非实有。离能所取，无别物故，非有实物，离二相故。是故一切，有为无为，若实若假，皆不离识。唯言，为遮离识实物，非不离识心所等法。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">诸识，自然是指三能变的八识<span lang="EN-US"> (含各各的心所) 。转变，即是由体起用，由识体变现出能缘的见分、和所缘的相分。能缘的见分为能分别，所缘的相分为所分别，以能分别的见分，分别所缘的相分，即是 ‘分别所分别’。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">这‘是诸识转变’的‘转变’二字，尚有下列三种意义：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 变现义：诸识的转变，是因转而变，因变而现。也就是由识体变现出见相二分，见分是能缘，即是见闻觉知，相分是所缘，即是根身器界，种种我相法相。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 变异义：变是生起，异是不同。由识体自证分生出见相二分，此见相二分，异于识体，故说是变异。再者，此见相二分，见分是能，相分是所，能所皆识体所变，而作用各异，故说是变异。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 改转义：是说由识体改转成见相二分，而有种种的我相或法相，由于具足这三种意义，所以说：‘是诸识转变’。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[由此彼皆无’ 者，此指的是能缘所缘的见分相分，彼指的是根身器界，种种我相法相。而此种种我法，都是能缘之心所变现。而能缘之心，也只是识体的作用。因此，若去掉这个识，不但没有外境的我相法相，也没有内境的见分相分。所以说，我人所认为一切的实我实法，不过是因缘和合的假有——也就是能缘所缘的见相二分而已。离开见相二分，即没有我法的存在；离开识，也没有见相二分的存在。故最终的结论是： ‘由此彼皆无，故一切唯识。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">二<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>心法生起缘由——由一切种识，如是如是变，以辗转力故，彼彼分别生。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">唯识家解释了上颂以后，外人复问难曰：<span lang="EN-US">‘若唯有识，都无外缘，何缘而生种种之分别？’意思是说：‘照你们唯识家所说，宇宙万有，只是相见二分的分别所分别，除识以外，没有实我实法的外境。既无外境，那么，能分别的处别心究竟缘何而生？这岂不是成了分别无因吗？]</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">为了解答这一问题，唯识家复说颂曰：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[由一切种识，如是如是变，以辗转力故，彼彼分别生。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">以上颂文，前二句明因，第三句明缘，第四句明所生的分别心。一切种识，指第八阿赖耶识。种是种子，色心诸法的种子，潜藏于第八识中，种子是第八识能生起万法的功能，以用从体，故曰一切种识。<span lang="EN-US">‘如是如是变’一句，变者，是潜隐的种子起现行，种子起现行，现行薰种子成为新种子，新种子复起现行，所谓：‘种子乍生现行，现行薰种子，三法辗转，因果同时。’ 这就是‘如是如是变’，也就是分别心生起之因。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[以辗转力故，彼彼分别生。’ 辗转是相资的意思，盖法不孤起，一法生起，须仗他法相资，种子起现行，也须要仗因托缘。盖有为法的生起，必依因缘和合。有因有缘，必然生果。因此，唯识学上立有 ‘六因、四缘、五果。’之说。事实上，因和缘没有什么差别，概略的说，因即是众缘之一，缘也是生果之因，不过在生起万法的关系条件上，因是较重要的一个条件而已。因此，六因之说，只是四缘的另一种分类方式。于此介绍四缘，四缘是因缘、等无间缘、所缘、增上缘，分述如下：</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 因缘<span lang="EN-US">： 因缘，是事物生起的众多关系条件中，具有生果能力的条件。经上说，‘谓有为法，亲自办果]， 称为因缘。但仅只有因仍不能生果，要因、缘具备才能生果。同时、在唯识学上的因缘，又不同于一般缘起的因缘。唯识学以 ‘万法唯识’立论，万法生起，皆是种子起现行的后果，因此，唯识学上的亲因缘， 就是第八阿赖耶识中含藏的种子。以种子生现行，始有宇宙万法。但‘法不孤起’ ，种子生现行，须要下列三缘具备。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 等无间缘<span lang="EN-US">： 等无间缘旧译次第缘，新译等无间，意思是‘密密迁移，等无间隙]，这是指我们的心识生起，念念生灭，刹那不停，前念心为后念心开导，引令后念心生起，前念为后念的缘，后念亦为前念的缘，次第生起，故亦称次第缘。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 所缘缘<span lang="EN-US">： 所缘缘旧译缘缘，这是心识攀缘外境的时候，此能攀缘之心，对所攀缘之境而生起，即是以境为其所缘。所缘缘这两个缘字，前一个缘是境，后一个缘是四缘之一的缘。语云：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[境由心生，心因境起。’心生之境是法境，属于心法，引心生起之境是外境，属于色法，二者全是心识攀缘的物件。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 增上缘<span lang="EN-US">： 增上是增加或加强的意思，对于一法的生起，有扶助之义，所以也称助缘。增上缘有顺益、违损两方面，自顺益方面说，能促成一法生起或成长者，称[与力增上缘’ ，不妨碍一法生生起或成长者，称‘不障增上缘’； 自违损方面说，此一法对他一法有妨害障碍者，如雨露是花木的顺益增上缘，而霜雹为花木的违损增上缘。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">唯识学是以<span lang="EN-US">‘万法唯识’立论，以一切法（色法及心法）的生起，皆是种子起现行的果，因此，种子是一切法的亲因缘，。再者，心法生起，要四缘具足； 色法生起，只须因缘与增上缘两种缘。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="color:#333399">三 <span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>有情相续缘由——由诸业习气，二取习气具，前异熟既尽，复生余异熟。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:#333399"></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
