<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[无得不思议，是出世间智，舍二粗重故，便证得转依。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">&lt;成唯识论&gt; 解释此颂曰：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[菩萨从见道起已，为断除余障证得转依，复数数修习无分别智。此智远离所取能取，故说无得及不思议，远离戏论，说为无得； 妙用难测，说不思议，是出世间无分别智，断世间故。名出世间。二取随眠，是世间本，唯此能断，独得出名。或出世名，依二义立，谓体无漏及证真如。此智俱斯二种义故，独名出世。余智不然，即十地中无中无分别智。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">无分别智，是一种能所两空，<span lang="EN-US">‘无智、亦无得’的空慧。这种空慧不可思议，是一种出世间的智慧，它能舍灭烦恼障及所知障的种子，以此而证得菩提及涅槃二转依果。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">颂文中<span lang="EN-US"> ‘舍二粗重故，便证得转依。’粗重二字，仍是种子的异名。‘转依’，是‘转染成净’。转者转舍，依者依止。转舍去染污的烦恼、所知二障，依止于涅槃、菩提二果。此亦称转识成智——转前五识为成所作智，转第六识为妙观察智，转第七识为平等性智，转第八识为大圆镜智。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">阿赖耶识摄持无漏有漏种子，修唯识行，以修持熏习力，舍有漏种子转为清净种子，至见道位，证二空真如。转染成净后的阿赖耶识，即转舍虚妄的识心，变为清净的智心。转依，即<span lang="EN-US">‘转其所依’，唯对‘所依’的看法， &lt;成唯识论’谓有二义：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 第一师义谓<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[依谓所依，即依他起，与染净法为所依故，染谓虚妄遍计所执，净谓真实圆成实性，转谓二分转舍转得。’ 据上所说，转依是由虚妄的依他起——即染分的阿赖耶识，转为净分的圆成实。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 第二师义谓<span lang="EN-US">：<span style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </span>[或依即是唯识真如，生死涅槃之所依故，愚夫颠倒迷此真如，故无始来受生死苦，圣者离倒悟此真如，便得涅槃毕竟安乐。’ 据第二义，谓依即是唯识真如，转舍迷妄颠倒的真如，转证悟的真如而得涅槃。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">转依，有能转道，所转依，所转舍，所转得四种意义。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 能转道：此即是能转舍二障、转得二果的智<span lang="EN-US"> (能转道的道、即是智。)此有二类：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、能伏道： 即是有漏无漏的加行、根本、后得三智，此智慧伏二障的种子势力而使其不生现行。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、能断道： 即是无漏的根本后得二智，此智慧断除二障的种子。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 所转依：即是能转之智，转舍染法，转得净法而成为所依，此亦有二类<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、持种依： 即是第八识，此识能任持染净诸法种子，故为所依，而使其转舍转得。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、迷悟依： 即是真如，若迷真如则生染法，悟之则生净法； 故为迷悟根本之所依，而使其转舍转得。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 所转舍：即是由能转道所转舍的有漏种子，此亦分为二类<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、所断舍： 断舍的即是烦恼所知二障种子。在无漏的真无间道生时，此类种子乃被断舍。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、所弃舍： 弃舍的即非障的有漏法、及劣无漏法的种子。这些虽不是障法、而不用断舍，但能持的第八识转为纯净圆明的时候，即不能任持此类种子，而自行将其弃舍。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 所转得：即是以能转道，转舍二障之因而转得者，此亦有二类<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">1、所显得： 显得者即真涅槃，断烦恼而显发者。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">2、所生得： 生得者即大菩提，断所知障而生起者。</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">五、 究竟位<span lang="EN-US">——此即无漏界，不思议善常，安乐解脱身，大牟尼名法。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">究竟位，是唯识修行五位中的最后一位。修行菩萨于第十地满心金刚喻定无间道，刹那之间，断尽二障种子，并于解脱道永舍劣无漏、及有漏诸法，以证菩提妙果。此即是圆满究竟位。三十颂曰<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:细明体">[此即无漏界，不思议善常，安乐解脱身，大牟尼名法。]</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">究竟位，事实上就是佛位，佛位是诸漏永尽，清净圆明，故称无漏。界是藏的意思，谓此中含藏无边希有大功德，故曰<span lang="EN-US">‘无漏界’。不思议者，佛之法身，不可执有，不可执无，离诸分别，绝诸戏论，故曰‘不思议’。善者微妙之净法，远离生死； 常者尽未来际，恒无变易。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">以上颂文，其中不思议、善、常、安乐，是二转依果体所具有的殊胜德性，是彰显究竟的无漏法界，兹分诠如下<span lang="EN-US">：</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">一、 不思议<span lang="EN-US">： 无漏界、离心缘相，故不可思； 离言说相，故不可议。亦即是二转依的果体——涅槃与菩提，甚深微妙，断绝寻思之境，不可以世间一切譬喻言议，故曰不思议</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">二、 善<span lang="EN-US">： 纯净法性，离诸烦恼。亦即谓清净法界的真涅槃，离生灭之法； 四智心品的大菩提，妙用无方，而二转依俱有顺益之相，与不善反，故成为善。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">三、 常<span lang="EN-US">： 二转依的果体，永不变灭，无有尽期。亦即是真涅槃无生无灭，性不变易；大菩提常住真如，为所依故，故成为常。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">四、 安乐<span lang="EN-US">： 清净法界，没有逼恼，亦能使所化有情安乐，故成其安乐。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span style="font-family:细明体">颂文<span lang="EN-US"> ‘解脱身大牟尼名法’者，解脱身是解脱烦恼障的缠缚而得到的果身。大牟尼、译为寂默。佛果的二障断除净尽，故名解脱身，亦名法身。法身是三身的总称，三身即自性身、受用身，变化身。</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5;mso-char-indent-size:12.0pt"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;</span></p>
